  1323. # [14:51] <Yoric> NeilAway: This is something that I intend to check carefully, as we depend on the semantics of chrome workers during shutdown.
  1324. # [14:51] <Yoric> However, my understanding is the following:
  1325. # [14:51] <Yoric> - chrome workers will finish handling waiting messages before they shut down;
  1326. # [14:52] * Joins: dbradley (dbradley@F13F4192.D4EBE3CD.8DD2BC91.IP)
  1327. # [14:52] <Yoric> - chrome workers will ignore any message posted once their shutdown is started;
  1328. # [14:52] <Yoric> - upon shutdown, chrome workers will run finalizers, which will in turn close any file left open.
  1329. # [14:52] <Yoric> Does this answer your question?
